Yereguwe n'Abanyarwanda mu gihe cy'icyerecyere cya BCE, Ibyaro Bigatanga ni kimwe mu bintu bishobora kuba bigwanjye byo kuba byatewe n'Abayivuga b'imidazolemu.
Ibi bikomeye mu Giza, cyangwa se "Giza Necropolis" mu mabere ya Misri y'Ibiraro, bifatika ibitaramo by'ipilikezi binyene (akaba igiterage cy'ipilikezi ari uko ariyo izeye), ibitaho by'imbuga bimwe, itagefurane twinyene, n’uyu mutwaro mutagatifu w'Igiza.
Iremere iruremye ryako ryatewe ku gutandika guhumba ubuwase Khufu, kandi imiduga n'ibiraro by'inshuro nke mirenge yashimwachungwa mu gushimangira imiryango n'ibanga by'umwami Khufu.
Isimbo rya "up bow" rirashaka "V", isimbo rya "down bow" rirashaka isoko cyangwa se akarere kaje kamo ubuzima bwayo.
Up అంటే మీరు చివర నుండి ప్రారంభించి, బాణాన్ని ముందుకు నెట్టాలి, మరియు కింద అంటే మీరు తడ్డంలో (మీ చేయి బాణాన్ని పట్టుకున్న చోట) ప్రారంభించి, బాణాన్ని వెనక్కి లాగాలి. Igihe cyo umara (Up) gitoreka ko uheanire ku icihe cy'inyoni,uvwxyzwe "tip" kandi ubureba umutwe w'ibanga, kandi umaganya ibanga. Igihe cyo umara (Down) gitoreka ko uheanire ku cyiro cy'ibanga (cyo uyaganya ibanga), kandi ubureba umutwe w'ibanga.
Urugabaga rurimo gusuma rushaka isuso rirambye, mu gihe urugabaga rurimo gusuma ruruka rurashakisha isuso rirambye kandi rurashashashye.
Shumbyi gufasha gukora imirurara yandikishwa ku isubazo, ariko remeza ko imirurara yandikishwa mu ntwaro irasobora umuziki, kandi yatekererwa cane.
Ubu bwa 6 Ukwaye 1789, Umwami Louis XVI ufite ishya, Ipimo Marie Antoinette, abana babo babiri bakuru (Marie Therese wari imyaka 11 na Louis-Charles wari imyaka 4), na Nyina w'Umwami, Madame Elizabeth, bafatirwa kwishura i Paris kwihirwe n'abahiri b'agomba.
Mu itzuki, bari bamaze gufanwa i Paris bari mu muto mushyushushye w'abantu bagasaba no kumashaka abahisemo ubutejwe n'ubwami bwabo.
Ubwete bw'abantu byateye amabaga y'Inyenzi na Sarah kugira amagurugi y'imoduka yari yaratewe.
Igihe kimwe, umwe mu bantu bari mu itsinda yashimangaga ikomo ry'umusore yagatikwe iVersailles, imbuso ye itari y'umutaganzalo, ahari imbere ye kwa Mutaganzalo yari yashatukijwe.
Gushoshuro za gihe cy'ubukuntu bw'Imperatiri y'Amerika mu guhungaburira yako mu Bubagi byagihe n'abaturage b'uBubagi bo kabamo.
Bwahesheje kwirerera amabaka ku itandaro ry'ubushabikere bw'Amerika bwashyize muri Repubulika ya Filipino, kugira ngo bayisabe umusoro mushya wa make n'ibishatshi by'ibihangano byarirwwe ku mpande z'ibihangano by'ibihangano byo ku Wall Street.
Urumuri, irindikiro rya kanyabushabakari riratetwe ku isenzu irimo gufashwa kwari abanyarwanda by'umwoko wa Filipino rizakubaka ibinyemerere by'ubupolitiki bw'Imperalisme by'Amerika.
Kuri ukwizemererwa kubona abasanzwe b'i Templar, ni ngutwereka amategeko y’inka yabagutsiye.
Ibi biri byari bitarajiwe byahise berekwa mu gihe cyo hari imiruriro myinshi, igihe cyo kwa Abaminuza bya gikinyarwanda, mu gihe cyo kuva mu gihe cy'umwaka 1000 kugeza mu gihe cy'umwaka 1300.
Ibi bihe bishimwa by’Igihe Cy’Impiro Cy’Amagacaca byarambiwe n’Igihe Cy’Impiro Cy’Amagacaca Kurambwa, kandi byarerejwe n’Igihe Cy’Impiro Cy’Amagacaca mu gihe gishatira 1500.
Urugambo rwa "technological determinism" ni ibisobanuro byinshi bikiri mu itumanaho, kwarwa ibintu bishobora gutuma itechnology itera ibizarwa (technology-push) cyangwa se ibyo bita "ubuzima bw'ihirwe bwayo" (technological imperative), kugeza ku intege nyiza yo kuba vita ko ubushwaho bw'abantu bwaratetwe n'amategeko y'inzira y'agaciro y'iza mpshyongiye n'uko izo mpshyongiye zivugwa muri technology.

Sundarbans zifite urusanso rwa kilometer iray'imbya 3,850, kuri rumwe rwa nyuma rishobora kuba mu majyendera/ibanga.
Kuvoye muri 1966, Sundarbans zo zari inyungaburarumabanga y’inyamashyye, kandi hasanwa ko ubu hari imashyye ya Serengeeti y’Ubwamerikirwa ingana n’imbarage 400 n’ibanza ku myambara y’agati ingana n’imbarage 30,000 muri iyi gese.
Ibi bisemburo bishatira imiryango y'ibihangano by'imidazole (by'imbere mu rugwaho rwa kivu) bibe bikora muri rusange ubwo by'agaciro muri rusange, ariko benshi, harimo abashatira ubutome bwa za Maghreb n'i Jakar/Bumthang, baragenda hagati ya 6h30 na 7h30.
Imbiswa n'uko ibicukiro by'imidazole runyine bisanzwa, ni iyihemba gutoreraho itike iminsi mikoranye.
Imyambara myinshi yashimba yagenewe ibicumbi bisukurwe bikuru by’uRubyogore b’Ubushorere bw’Ahanu, zigana n’izimanwa zitari zikabaye zirambwachungupamo.
